Marker Color Codes

Red = Location
Orange = AMV
Yellow = Scenario
White = PS4 Scenario
Green = AnimScene
Magenta = PersChar
Black = Waypoint Record
Gray = Vehicle Record
Blue = Script Coordinate
Purple = IPL
Light Blue = Miscellanous
